<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若依據與眼根和合不相離的色法而言，則有七種物類，包括眼根以及身體，因為眼睛依止在身體上面；而且是堅硬性的地大所成；眼根還有顏色；也有香氣，還有觸。根據不相離攝來說，眼相有七物，就是眼、身、地、色、香、味、觸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、界攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科界攝，界是種子，以構成眼根的種子而言，有十種物類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若皆據界攝，則有十物。即此七物界及水、火、風界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　就界攝的種子而言，形成眼根的種子有十種物類，就是眼、身、地、色、香、味、觸及水、火、風界這十物的種子，形成眼根。〈本地分‧意地〉卷3說過：一切色法，都是由地、水、火、風四大種所成，眼根雖以地大為自相，其實它也含有水、火、風大種在內，依據不相離攝有七物；依據界攝，則有十物。地、水、火、風任何一種物質看起來雖然只有地一種，可是裡面有其它的種子，根據這個道理說界攝。事實上因緣一轉變水、火、風的作用就能現前，因為有某功能性，表示有相對應色法種類之種子的緣故。如果就界攝，地、水、火、風都是互相有其他的種子的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、例餘根2　酉一、例同</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘根，以眼根為例，耳、鼻、舌、身根等也是一樣，分二科；第一科例同，推理可見緣起的道理，法法相因，法法相依。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如眼，耳、鼻、舌當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如眼根以界攝有十種，耳根、鼻根和舌根也是一樣；若依據相攝只有一種，耳識、鼻識、舌識所依的清淨色。以不相離攝有七種，將眼換成耳、鼻、舌。如果根據界攝再加上水、火、風共有十個。其它諸根也是一樣的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、顯別2　戌一、耳鼻舌根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯別，各別顯示出來其它特別的情況，分二科；第一科耳鼻舌根，說出耳、鼻、舌這三種根的差別相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="54p4314"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中差別者，謂耳、耳識所依清淨色，鼻、鼻識所依清淨色，舌、舌識所依清淨色。餘如前說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此中的差別，是指耳是耳識所依的清淨色，鼻是鼻識所依清淨色，舌是舌識所依清淨色。餘是不相離攝及界攝，就如同前面所說的眼根一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》餘如前說者：不相離攝，名之為餘。耳、鼻、舌三，如前眼說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不相離攝，名之為餘，其實包括界攝。耳、鼻、舌三的情形，如前眼根所說的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、身根2　亥一、不相離等攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科身根，各別顯示身根，身體的情況，分二科；第一科不相離等攝，說明不相離等攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若身，當除眼等四。何以故？由遠離彼獨可得故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　身體的不相離攝應該除去眼、耳、鼻、舌這四個法。為什麼呢？因為若沒有眼睛、耳朵、鼻子、舌頭，身體可以單獨存在。如果依據不相離攝，身體就包括身根是地大所成的，也包含其它色、香、味、觸等。身根是六法所攝，就是身、地、色、香、味、觸。還有一個情況，就是初投胎時，剛開始只有父精母血和合的一小滴身根而已，雖然眼睛、耳朵、鼻子，還沒有長出來，身根還是可以自己存在的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若身當除眼等四等者：前說眼、耳、鼻、舌不離於身，是故說身不相離攝。然非此身不離眼、耳、鼻、舌，是故不說眼、耳、鼻、舌不相離攝。由是故言當除眼等四。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說眼、耳、鼻、舌不離於身，所以說身屬於不相離攝。但並非身不離眼耳鼻舌，說到身根的不相離攝時，就不提眼、耳、鼻、舌這四法了。所以才說應該除掉眼、耳、鼻、舌這四法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、相攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科相攝，約相攝來討論身根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此相者，謂身識所依清淨色。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　身識所依止的清淨色根，是身根，這是相攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、外色2　申一、略辨攝2　酉一、色香味觸</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科外色，以下分別色、聲、香、味、觸五種外色，分二科；第一科略辨攝，要略的說明色、香、味、觸這四法相攝的情形，又分二科；第一科色香味觸，說明色香味觸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於外色、香、味、觸彼所行相中，除一切根，餘一切如前應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若就眼等五根之外的色、香、味、觸，分別為眼鼻舌身及眼鼻舌身識所行相中，不包括內五根，其餘相攝的情形例前可知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="54p4315"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》除一切根餘一切如前應知者：當知此說於外色、香、味、觸不相離攝，非一切根俱為所行，是故除之。唯彼四相決定可得，名餘一切如前應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是指色、香、味、觸不相離攝，色、香、味、觸的認知，各有所相應的眼、鼻、舌、身根，並非一切內根都能取色、香、味、觸，因而簡除不算在內。以相攝而言，只有色、香、味、觸這四種相一定可得。其它的就像前面所說，色、香、味、觸彼此都能互相相攝。色法裡面一定有香、味、觸；香法裡面一定也有色、味、觸；味裡面一定有色、香、觸；觸裡面也有色、香、味。每一法都包括四法，只有這四相決定可得，其它不一定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、聲及聲界2　戌一、標說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科聲及聲界，以下討論聲的現行及聲的種子，聲音要有因緣才會現起，沒有因緣不會現起，分二科；第一科標說，標示說明出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">聲及聲界不恆有故，今當別說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　聲音與聲的種子，不會常常有的。要有因緣才有，現在另外來說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、辨攝2　亥一、聲</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨攝，說明聲音所攝的範圍，分二科；第一科聲，說明聲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於是處有聲，當知此處復增其一。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以色法的不相離攝而言，如果這個地方有聲音，就應該要增加上聲這個法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、聲界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科聲界，說明聲的種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">應知聲界，一切處增。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　就種子而言，一切法中都有聲的種子。比如說眼根以不相離攝有七物，以界攝有十物，如果加上聲界就有十一個，意思就是這樣。這裡稍微複雜一點，以聲界，一切處就增加了聲界。如果是聲音，只是有因緣時才加上，若沒有因緣就不算在內。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》聲及聲界不恆有故等者：聲相間斷，由現緣生，名不恆有。若於前說不相離攝，隨一彼色聚中有聲可得，即說彼聚聲亦不相離攝。由是當知，復增其一。若據界攝，即彼聲界一切處增。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　聲是有間斷的，有因緣才能夠出現。不像色、香、味、觸是一直存在的，只要有色法就有色、香、味、觸。在前面所說的不相離攝，眼耳鼻舌身、色香味觸的不相離攝中，隨其中一種色聚中若有聲音的話，就說那個色聚不相離攝包括聲了。由此可知，這裡說復增其一，就是此義。不相離攝本來沒有包括聲音，現在再加一個聲，這是復增其一。如果根據界攝，以種子觀點來討論相攝，一切法裡面都應該還要加上聲界，因為一切法都可能有聲音的。若燒火時也有聲音，碰撞時也有聲音，風一吹也有聲音，地、水、火、風的變化，通通都有聲音。所以若以界攝，一切眼耳鼻舌身、色香味觸，都可以再加上聲界。這裡只是略辨外色，下面是對外色的廣分別，還有詳細的說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、廣分別2　酉一、指色等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣分別，詳細分別色、聲、香、味、觸等，分二科；第一科指色等，指出色等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，色等所緣境界，如本地分已廣分別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，色、聲、香、味、觸等所緣境界，在〈本地分〉已經說了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="54p4316"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如本地分已廣分別者：謂意地中建立一種色乃至觸，後復漸增建立十種，名廣分別應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/03.htm#42109:2275">陵本三卷十一頁241</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈本地分‧意地〉卷3，103~104頁中，建立一種色乃至一種觸，後又漸漸增加乃至十種色、聲、香、味、觸，這是廣分別應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、辨觸處2　戌一、別釋相2　亥一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨觸處，分別觸處，分二科；第一科別釋相，各別解釋觸的相狀，又分二科；第一科標，標出來觸的範圍。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="52888:42111"></a><a name="246:42111"></a>若觸處中所說造色滑乃至勇，當知即於大種分位假施設有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　觸到造色的各種觸覺中，滑乃至勇，都是地、水、火、風四大種分位的狀態，假施設而有的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋16　天一、滑性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，雖然有二十種觸，歸納成十六科，分十六科；第一科滑性，大種清淨性，稱滑性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂於大種清淨性，假立滑性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以地水火風的清淨性，假立為滑。地水火風清淨，才能夠滑。地板如果擦得很乾淨就會滑。像佛的皮膚很滑，蚊子都停不住，一上去就溜滑掉了。凡夫的皮膚很粗，蚊蠅上去就能停得住。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、重性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科重性，大種堅實性，稱重性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於大種堅實性，假立重性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　地水火風很堅硬、實在，這是重性。這人身體很重、很結實、很堅固，也稱為重。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、澀性及輕性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科澀性及輕性，大種不清淨假立澀性，不堅實假立輕性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於大種不清淨、不堅實性，假立澀性及輕性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　澀是有點粗躁義。地水火風不大清淨，是不滑，這是澀性。與重性相反的不堅實是輕性。重是堅實的，不堅實是輕性，這些都是假安立的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天四、軟性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科軟性，大種不清淨，慢緩性假立為軟性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於大種不清淨、慢緩性，假立軟性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　地水火風不清淨，而且慢緩時假立為軟性。比如說，覺得全身軟趴趴的沒有力氣，就是自己的地水火風不夠清淨，沒有力量，而且很慢緩提不起勁了，這是軟性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天五、冷</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科冷，水與風和合生，假立為冷。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由水與風和合生故，假立有冷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　水與風在一起，有冷的感覺，這也是假安立的。在冷的地方容易得風濕，因為冷就是因為有水有風，就有風寒，所以感覺冷。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="54p4317"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天六、饑渴弱力</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科饑渴弱力，饑餓、口渴、及羸弱的體力。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由闕任持不平等故，假立饑渴及弱力。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於闕乏食物的任持，支持身體的養分不平衡，這個時候肚子餓了，假立為饑。水分不夠口渴了，假立為渴。體力衰弱，就名為弱力，沒有力量了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天七、彊力及飽</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科彊力及飽，彊大的力量及飽食的感覺。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由無所闕無不平等故，假立彊力及飽。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於食物無所缺乏，地水火風平衡沒有不平等的情況，這時身體感覺強而有力，肚子感覺吃飽了，以此假立彊力及飽。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天八、病</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科病，由於地水火風不平等，而且有變化，令身體錯亂，假立為病。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由不平等變異錯亂不平等故，假立病。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於地水火風不平等，而且有變化，令身體錯亂，假立為生病。身體火大過盛就有火氣；風大問題能引起手或頭顫動不停，或行動不便；地大過盛引起肥胖；水大過盛引起水腫。這些都是病，形容身體四大不平等的情況，所以病是假安立的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天九、老</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科老，由時分變異不平等，假立老。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由時分變異不平等故，假立老。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於時間的改變，諸根變異衰弱不平等時，假立為老。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天十、死</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科死，由於命根變異不平等，假立為死。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由命根變異不平等故，假立死。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於命根變異不平等，這時四大分離，不能存活，假立為死。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天十一、癢</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科癢，由血有過患不平等，假立癢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由血有過患不平等故，假立癢。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於血有過患不平等的原因。當靜坐時，有時覺得身上有螞蟻在爬，感覺臉部或哪裡會有癢的感覺，就是氣血不平順。當血有過患不平等，通不過去時就會癢，由此假立為癢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天十二、悶絕</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十二科悶絕，暈倒是悶絕，由於飲食不恰當、不平等故，假立悶絕。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="54p4318"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由惡飲食不平等故，假立悶絕。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　吃錯食物，地水火風不平等，會暈倒，以此假立悶絕。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天十三、黏</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十三科黏，黏的感覺，由地與水和合生，假立黏。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由地與水和合生故，假立黏。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　地大與水大和合時，假立為黏。當身體流汗時，地和水合在一起，會有黏的感覺。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天十四、疲極</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十四科疲極，疲勞的感覺，由往來勞倦不平等，假立疲極。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由往來勞倦不平等故，假立疲極。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　疲勞就是因為來來去去，如果常常出外，就算坐車，也會覺得很疲勞。常常來來回回的走動，就會有疲勞。這是形容身體的感受，所以疲勞也是假立的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天十五、憩息</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十五科憩息，休息，遠離往來勞倦，假立憩息。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若遠離彼，由平等故，假立憩息。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由遠離往來勞倦的不平等，身體休息夠了，四大平等，假立為憩息。修菩薩道中有一個很重要的力量，就是休息力，菩薩一定要休息，才能繼續作利益眾生的事情。一個人如果不休息，身體很快就搞挎，就不能再繼續作了，所以休息也很重要。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天十六、勇銳</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十六科勇銳，勇猛銳利，由除垢等離萎顇，假立勇銳。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由除垢等離萎顇故，假立勇銳。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除去身體的骯髒，遠離憔悴時，感覺這人很勇銳，很有精神，這也是形容身體的狀態，而假立勇銳。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="54p4319"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若觸處中所說造色滑乃至勇等者：集論中說：何等所觸一分？謂四大種所造身根所取義。謂滑性、澀性、輕性、重性、軟性、緩、急、冷、饑、渴、飽、力、劣、悶、癢、黏、病、老、死、疲、息、勇。（集論一卷三頁）今於此中，闕無緩急，弱力即劣，餘一切同。假施設義，如文可知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《集論》中說：什麼是所觸的一分呢？能造的地、水、火、風四大種所造的身根，所取的境界。身根所取的包括滑性、澀性、輕性、重性、軟性、緩、急、冷、饑、渴、飽、力、劣、悶、癢、黏、病、老、死、疲、息、勇這幾種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《集論》卷1中沒有解釋緩跟急。弱力就是《集論》說的劣。其餘的義理二論相同，假施設的道理，如前面所說的文可以知道。急、緩二種，這裡沒有說到。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《集論》卷1中說有二十二種，這裡只說二十種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、略攝位2　亥一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科略攝位，將觸處要略歸納成六位，分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是一切，說諸大種總有六位。謂淨不淨位、堅不堅位、慢緩位、和合位、不平等位、平等位。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　根據以上所說，諸大種可以歸納成六位：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、淨不淨位：淨位指大種清淨性，如滑性、勇銳等；不淨位指大種不清淨性，如澀性、輕性、軟性等。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、堅不堅位：堅的就是重性；不堅的就是澀性和輕性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、慢緩位就是軟性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、和合位：如冷與黏，就是由水和風和合而生的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、不平等位：如饑渴、弱力、病、悶絕、和疲極。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、平等位：如強力、飽、還有憩息。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是另一種分類法，便於進一步了解二十種觸，都是形容身體的感覺，都是四大種的分位差別，所以都是假安立的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、開合</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科開合，說明六位開成八位，合成六位，平等平等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是六位，復開為八。若八、若六，平等平等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這六位也可以開展成八位。分成八種或六種，內容都不出二十種觸，所以八種或六種是平等平等的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如是六位復開為八者：淨不淨位、堅不堅位，各復開二，是故成八。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六位怎麼樣開為八位的呢？淨不淨位開展為淨位及不淨位，堅不堅位也開展成堅位及不堅位，這樣就有四位，再加上慢緩位、和合位、不平等位、與平等位，總共就有八位。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、總料簡5　未一、辨所識2　申一、二識所識</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前一科顯出內色與外色的差別，第二科總料簡，將色類總合起來思惟簡別一番，分五科；第一科辨所識，分別這些色法是那一類識所認知的，又分二科；第一科二識所識，說明色乃至觸都是自識及意識所識。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，一切色乃至觸，皆二識所識，謂自識所識及意識所識。或漸、或頓。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　再說，一切色、聲、香、味、觸都有二種識來了別。前五識緣取外五境，就是這裡所說的自識所識，加上意識與前五識一起活動，作進一步的了別；比如說色法是眼識所識，以及意識所識，意識一定會跟著一起活動，作進一步的分別。聲是耳識所識及意識所緣，香是有鼻識及意識所識，味是舌識及意識所識，觸就是身識及意識所識。或漸、或頓，前六轉識各別單取一類的色相，這是漸；六轉識總合頓取種種差別色相，就是頓。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、意識所識</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科意識所識，意識能了別五根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">眼等五根，一意識所識。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼等五根，眼、耳、鼻、舌、身等五根，只有意識能了別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="54p4320"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》或漸或頓者：謂如眼識，於一時間，於一事境唯取一類無異色相；或於一時，頓取非一種種色相。乃至廣說身識，或於一時，於一事境唯取一類無異觸相；或於一時，頓取非一種種觸相。如是分別意識，於一時間，或取一境相，或取非一種種境相。義如前說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/51.htm#42160:39538">陵本五十一卷八頁4086</a>）此應準知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或漸或頓是這樣解釋，比如有時只有眼識緣取一類沒有差別的色相；有時一眼看去同時看到很多的色相，如花、草、樹木，這是頓，乃至身識也是一樣。或於一時，於一事境只有取一類的無異觸相，比如現在只有接觸硬的感覺。或者是一時同時感覺觸到各式各樣冷、軟、澀、滑等，這是頓。意識也是一樣，如是分別意識，於一時間，或者是取一個境相為所緣境；或者是取得多種的境相，這是頓。頓是指識同時緣取不同類的所緣境相；漸是指識一次只有取一類所緣境相。如〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷51，1695頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、辨有無3　申一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨有無，分別色界中色法的有無，分三科；第一科標，標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，色界中無現香、味，然有彼界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　再說，色界天中，沒有現行的香跟味，因為他們沒有段食，不須要使用鼻識及舌識，不必像欲界有情這樣吃三餐，他們是以禪悅為食，以禪定就可以資養色身，不用吃飯，也不必像欲界有情還要去買菜、買米，也沒有開門七件事，因此他們沒有鼻識舌識，也沒有現行的香味，可是還有香味的種子。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此二皆是段食攝故。由無此二，鼻、舌二識亦無。此就現行說，非就界說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　香、味二種都是段食。色界沒有香、味二種現行，也沒有鼻舌二識。鼻、舌二識在色界天沒有作用，為了莊嚴，為了好看，但是他們還是有鼻子和舌頭，但是沒有作用。這是就現行來說，沒有香及味這件事，生到那裡去，就不用吃飯了。就種子來說，還是有香及味的種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、辨假實2　申一、標蘊攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科辨假實，分別色法的假實差別，分二科；第一科標蘊攝，標出內外色都是色蘊所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是一切色蘊所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這一切內色的眼、耳、鼻、舌、身，以及外色的色、聲、香、味、觸，都是屬於色蘊所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、辨差別3　酉一、九種色</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨差別，說明色蘊所攝法的假實差別，分三科；第一科九種色，九種色屬實有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="54p4321"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">色中九種是實物有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有九種色是實物有，包括眼耳鼻舌身及色聲香味。詳細分別五根及色聲香味，其實其中還是有假有與實有的差別，但是略而不說。由於觸範圍廣，假實差別比較明顯，假有的很多，實有的比較少，所以特別將它列出來。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色法：青黃赤白是實有。長短方圓大小，只是用來形容色法的形狀，是假有，沒有真實的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　聲：有執受大種聲與不執受大種聲是實有。好聽或不好聽聲，也是形容聲音的，都是假有的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　香：眾法和合所生的是實有。好的香、或者是壞的香，這類的差別是識的分別，都屬於假有。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　味：苦、酢（酸）、鹹、淡、甜、辣等，是實有。其餘好不好吃這一類，可意味、不可意味等屬於假有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、觸所攝色2　戌一、是實有</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科觸所攝色，身觸所攝四大種所造假色，分二科；第一科是實有，說明實有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">觸所攝中，四大種是實物有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　攝屬於觸的色法中，四大種，就是地水火風之堅濕暖動四種物性，四大種是能造，能造的是實物有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、唯假有</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科唯假有，除四大種是實物有其餘種類的觸都是假有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知所餘唯是假有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其它如滑、勇、堅等，都屬於假有。前面說過的二十種法也都是假有的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》當知所餘唯是假有者：此說所觸一分滑乃至勇應知。唯於大種分位假施設有，故是假有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說到所觸的一分，能觸的四大種地水火風是實有的，所觸的滑乃至勇，只是在地水火風四大種的分位假施設而有，所以說是假有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、墮法處色2　戌一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科墮法處色，意處所緣的境界是法，法處所攝色也有實有及假有，分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">墮法處色亦有二種，謂實有、假有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　墮法處色又名法處所攝色，即意識所緣的色，有實有和假有二種。五俱意識初剎那，與五識同緣現量時，說它是實有；第二念依名言而取相分別，是假有的。色法分成十一種，包括五根、五塵，還有一分法處所攝色，一共有十一種。法處所攝色有各種不同說法，如果根據後文，包括律儀色、不律儀色、還有大威德定所行色，這三種。《成唯識論》中說有五種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、極略色：將色法分析到最小的單位，就是極微，也就是極略色。是意識所緣的假色，唯是意識的虛妄分別，不是真實有那個最小的單位。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、極迥色：分析空界的色法如明、暗等，沒有質礙性的色法，分析到最小不可分割的單位；或顯色至遠而為難見，是名極迥色。極迥色也是一種意識所緣的色法，不是實法，也是假色。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、受所引色：受所引色是指戒體。佛弟子受戒時觀想十方法界清淨妙善的戒法，由頭頂灌入身心成為戒體，又稱無表色。這也是假安立的法，依思心所種子的分位而安立的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、遍計所起色：就是凡夫平常的境界，第六意識的影像色。五俱意識第二剎那，前一剎那的現量過了，第二念第六意識開始依名言認識，這是桌子、椅子、人等，在心裡所現出來的影像色，都是遍計所起色。非實計實，也是假有的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、定自在所生色：定自在所生色是定果色，由定力所變現出來的色法，通於凡聖所變。八地以上菩薩所變的一定是實色，凡夫的定境裡面只能變出假色，所以定自在所生色可以通於假實。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、隨釋2　亥一、實有</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，解釋實有及假有的法處所攝色，分二科；第一科實有，說明實有的法處所攝色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有威德定所行境，猶如變化，彼果、彼境及彼相應識等境色，是實物有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是有屬於無漏的威德定，這是聖人的定。本論前文說大阿羅漢及八地以上菩薩才有大威德定。大威德定所變現的境界，好像是神通變化一樣。變是指原有的事物轉變一番；化就是沒有的事物轉變成有。大威德定所緣的境界及意識相應的境色，都是屬於實物有。聖人的大威德定，馬上就可以現出來真實的色法。比如他想蘋果，馬上可以現出一個真實的蘋果。如果凡夫想蘋果，只是一個名字而已。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="54p4322"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若有威德定所行境等者：思所成慧地決擇中說：又根本定，名具威德三摩地，此色是彼所緣，非餘。譬如非一切心皆能變化，若所有心具大威德方能成辦，非所餘心。此亦如是，要具威德極靜定心，方能為緣生此無見無對諸色。此如化色，亦非不具大威德心及不定心所緣境界，但是彼心所緣境界。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/65.htm#42183:51754">陵本六十五卷十頁5183</a>）由是當知，此色定果所生定所行境，是名彼果彼境。是定相應意識及諸心所所緣境界，名彼相應識等境色。為簡此色不為清淨色根所取，亦不為依彼清淨色識所緣，故作是說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈決擇‧思所成慧地〉卷65，2084頁中說：初禪到四禪的根本定，稱為具威德三摩地。實有的法處所攝色，不是其他色聲等諸色，這是根本定所緣。譬如不是所有的定心都能變化神通，只有具四禪以上大威德的定心，才有變化神通的能力，不是其他的定心。此實有的法處所攝色也是一樣，要有具威德的極靜定心，才能緣生此種欲界看不到且沒有質礙的色法。實有的法處所攝色，就如神通所變化的色法，也不是不具大威德定心或不具定心等所緣的境界，只有具大威德定的心，才能夠緣慮到這種色法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由此應當可以了知，此實有的法處所攝色，是根本定所生果，是根本定所行境界，因此稱為彼果彼境。此實有的法處所攝色，是根本定相應的意識及相應的各種心所所緣的境界，因此稱為彼相應識等境色。為了簡除此實有的法處所攝色不同於欲界眼、耳、鼻、舌、身五根所取的清淨色，也不是依彼清淨色根所發五識所緣的色，所以才這樣說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、假有</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科假有，說明假有色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若律儀色、不律儀色，皆是假有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　善戒的戒體及惡戒體，都是假有。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若律儀色等者：此假有義前已決擇，應知依彼律儀、不律儀思而假立故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　律儀色就是受戒時成就的善戒體。不律儀色是說有一種人發願做殺生等事，他有惡戒，惡戒也有惡戒的體，就是不律儀色。會成為戒體，就是因為有強烈的誓願及期限才能成就戒體，這些都是假有的，是依思心所而假立的。如果一個人作善或者是作惡時，沒有很強的誓願及期限，不能說是律儀色或不律儀色，這種人他沒有什麼強烈的心情去造善、或造惡，就是非律儀非不律儀色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、辨定色4　申一、明界繫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科辨定色，說明勝定果色，是在定中所變現出來的色法，是意識所緣的色法，分四科；第一科明界繫，說明定所行色的界繫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又定所行色，若依此繫定，即由此繫大種所造。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又定自在所生色，依定所繫的界地，比如說是色界，隨著所屬界地，就由此界繫之大種所造。此處說大種所造，不是指大種所生，如下文1793頁說：法處所攝勝定果色，當知此色唯依勝定不依大種，然從緣彼種類影像三摩地發故，亦說彼大種所造，非依彼生故名為造。例如在定外看見青坐具，後入定中觀察所見青，當定心現出青色影像，是彼本質青坐具之類，也說從彼坐具大種所造，事實上並非依彼大種所造所生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　據窺基大師《瑜伽師地論略纂》卷14說：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、若約本質功能，如〈決擇‧思所成慧地〉卷66所說：隨緣彼界，彼界大種造。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、若據親生，即定中所變大種造。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、若據由生，即是定力，非由大種。如是種種依義差別也。又也通無色界，有此威德定色。此處說隨定所繫，這是根據唯在色界，因為色界定慧均等定很明利故，因此論說：依此定即此繫四大造。若無色界也如前〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉53，1762頁所說：色邊際有二種，一種是下界的欲纏色，一種是中界的色纏色。這是以業增上所生諸色，說無色界無有諸色，不是以勝定自在色說。因為由彼勝定於一切色皆得自在，諸定加行能令現前，若是無色界的勝定自在色名極微細定所生色。所以本卷1781頁說：「心自在轉微細性者，謂色無色二界諸色。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　定所行色，是定自在所生色。據窺基大師《大乘法苑義林章》卷5：勝定果色章說，此色有通凡聖所起，道理如下：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、 有人主張此色通凡聖起，原因是：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 本卷1781，說：心自在轉微細性，是指色無色二界諸色。如《契經》說：有平等心天，曾於人中薰瑩心故，隨此修力住一毛端空量地處，展轉更互不相妨礙。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 又阿含云：無色諸天淚下如雨，佛邊側立。如是等證處處皆有。彼處既說上二界天現身住此，又說此色也通有漏，本卷1780頁說：又此定色但是世間，有漏無漏由定而生。由此可知凡聖皆能現起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3.《顯揚聖教論》唯說諸佛菩薩能現，據大威德勝人說故，怎可說二乘等也不能變，因為《增壹阿含經》卷18說：「尊者舍利弗入滅時無色天，淚下如春月細雨。」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　4. 本卷1780頁說：又復此色雖非出世定之所行，然由彼定增上力故，有一能現者，論說聖者具有世間出世間智（後得智），顯示不是出世間無分別智之所行，並不是簡別異生不能現起，因此可知此色定通凡聖。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、 有人主張此色非異生凡夫所起，原因是：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 《顯揚聖教論》卷18說：「法處所攝色，略說有十二種相。一影像相、二所作成就相、三無見相、四無對相、五非實大種所生相、六屬心相、七世間相、八不可思議相、九世間三摩地果相、十出世間三摩地果相、十一自地下地境界相、十二諸佛菩薩隨心自在轉變不可思議相。其中唯說諸佛菩薩等變能變現不可思議之定自在所生實色。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 本卷1780頁又說：雖非出世定之所行，然由彼定增上力故，有一能現。尚非一切聖者能起，何況凡夫？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 〈決擇‧思所成慧地〉卷65，2085頁說：要具威德極靜定心，方能為緣生此定色；亦非不具大威德心，及不定心，所緣境界，豈是異生類能獲威德極靜定心現起諸色？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　4. 本卷1780頁又說：此事不可思議。若異生起應思議所攝，由此唯聖非凡所起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、結語：〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷33說：「諸聖神通隨所變事，隨所作事，隨所勝解，一切皆能如實成辦，無有改異，堪任有用；非聖神通不能如是，猶如幻化，唯可觀見，不堪受用」。因此前一種解釋為是。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若依此繫定等者：地繫差別種種非一，隨所依止，即彼大種所造。如是應知定所行色差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　界地所繫差別種類很多，各各不同，隨其所依止的界地，由彼界地的地水火風所造，由此可知勝定所行色的差別。玄奘大師說，這裡特別是說色界定，欲界沒有這樣的功能。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、出體性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科出體性，說明定所行色的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又此定色但是世間，有漏、無漏由定而生，非出世間。由此定色，有戲論行定為因故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又定果色是屬於世間俗諦所攝，是由禪定力所變現之色法，通於凡聖所變，凡夫所變為有漏色，聖人所變為無漏色；《瑜伽論記》卷14，景法師說：這是說明這種定所行色，唯是聖人定所生色，不是凡夫，但又說：地前菩薩涅槃心滿加行心中亦得顯現義故是有漏，地前菩薩後無漏心即現是無漏；窺基大師說：若菩薩是無漏，若二乘是有漏，都能變化令他受用，是聖人後得智世間心所現，因此名為世間。不是聖人出世間根本無分別智的境界，不屬於第一義諦。因為出世間第一義諦是言語道斷，心行處滅，根塵識、器世間、能所、語言皆不現的無分別境。由定果色，是凡聖在定中依於名言戲論為因勝解所成，屬世間，不是出世間第一義諦的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="54p4323"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》有漏無漏由定而生者：此漏無漏，謂彼色類應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　定果色有屬於有漏的和無漏的情況，有漏色是凡夫所變現的；無漏色是聖人所變現的。因此說勝定果色可以通於凡聖，所變現出來的定果色也有不同。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、簡功能2　酉一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科簡功能，簡別定果色的功能，分二科；第一科標，標出並非所有定心能起變化。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又非一切所有定心皆有能生此色功能，唯一類有如能起化。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　並不是所有定心都具有能生出定果色的功能，只有一類具大威德根本定者才能夠生出實有的定果色。猶如神通能變化出各種色法，但不是每一個具有神通者都能變現出實有的化色，唯一類聖神通者，才具有生出實有化色的功能。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》唯一類有如能起化者：唯根本定具大威德，能生此色，名一類有。猶如化色，非不具有大威德心能成辦故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　只有一類成就根本定，具有大威德力，才能夠生出實有的定果色，稱為一類有。猶如依神通所變現的實有色法，並不是所有定心都能變化，唯有根本定具大威德的聖者人才能夠成辦。《顯揚聖教論》中分別說，大威德心是八地以上菩薩的境界。關於定果色有種種的說法，窺基大師歸納成以下二種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種約定色而說，通於凡聖。凡夫或聖人依定力都能變現出色法。例如經典上說，舍利弗尊者入滅時，無色界天的人淚如雨下，好像春天的雨下下來，無色界天的人並非聖人，可是有定自在所生色，所以還是可以流淚，因此定果色，通於有色無色界及凡聖；不一定聖人才有辦法變現出真實色法，凡夫有高深禪定的人也可以。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種約化色而說，有人主張一定要八地以上菩薩才有這個能力，若是八地菩薩變現出錢一百萬，則一百萬是可以用的。如果是八地以下菩薩，變的就沒有用了。無著菩薩的《顯揚聖教論》主張要八地以上的菩薩變現的勝定果色才有真實的相用。不過他認為，定果色應該是通於凡聖，因為根據本文說有漏、無漏，由定而生。是指所變現出來的色類為有漏色或無漏色。有漏色是凡夫所變現的；無漏色是聖人所變現的，因此說勝定果色可以通於凡聖。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、釋2　戌一、能生色</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋定果色的功能，分二科；第一科能生色，說明何種功能才能夠生勝定果色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂不思惟，但由先時作意所引，離諸闇昧，極善清淨明了現前，當知是定乃能生色。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如何生出定果色呢？若所得定不用特別去思惟。在入定之前，先有作意要這樣子變現。他的心很光明，沒有黑暗，非常的清淨，定心非常的穩定，他的定色很明白的現前，由此了知此種定是可以生出色法的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》離諸闇昧等者：此顯修習光明定者離諸定難。應知由彼諸難能障三摩地相令不清淨明了現前故。定難差別有十一種，如三摩呬多地說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/12.htm#42200:10060">陵本十二卷十三頁1021</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡是顯示修習光明定的人，遠離了疑等種種的定難。這些種種的定難能夠使得三摩地定的相貌不清淨，不能明了現前。定難差別有十一種，依思所成，乃至修所成的定有十一種不同的定難。如〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷12，421頁所說定難差別。在〈本地分‧修所成地〉卷20的726~728頁中，特別提出來十一種定難，對治去除這些定難才能夠得到禪定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、不能生色</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不能生色，說明有一種定是不能生出定果色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若定力勵數數思惟，假勝解力而得見者，當知不能生起此色。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果入這個定，要很努力的思惟，假藉勝解力，才能現出色法，則不能變現出定果色。欲界的人如果很勉強的才能入定，就不能變現出有用的定果色了。這裡看得出來色界天以上的人，他們定力很強，能任運的入定。入定前先作意，想看到什麼？馬上就現出來。一般人是沒辦法，連入未到地定都很困難，雖然一直努力在所緣境上，但心馬上會流散，即使數數思惟還不能入定，這種定是不能變現出定果色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="54p4324"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申四、明增上</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科明增上，說明有一類得定自在佛菩薩，能不以戲論行為因而生勝定果色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又復此色，雖非出世定之所行，然由彼定增上力故，有一能現。當知此事不可思議。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又雖然勝定果色不是出世間定所變現的，但是定自在菩薩得到無分別智以後，由根本智的增上力量為基礎，他的後得智也能夠現出一類特殊的勝定果色，這是定自在菩薩的境界，不可思議。換言之，這一類聖者菩薩沒有戲論行為因，也能夠變現色法，這種境界就不是凡夫能夠所想像出來的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》有一能現者：此說得定自在諸佛菩薩，不由有戲論行為因，隨其所欲，能現此色故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處說得定自在的諸佛菩薩，不是由戲論行的因緣而現定色，他的後得智能夠隨其所欲自在變現定色。前面「申二、出體性」文中提及定果色是有戲論行為因，所以其體性是屬於世間的。這裡論主特別簡別出來，有一類得定自在的諸佛菩薩，是不可思議的境界，可以經由無漏定增上，不以有戲論行（有漏定）為因而生此勝定果色。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《雜集論述記》卷2說：有一能現，是說聖者具有世間出世間智，顯示不是出世智之所行，並非簡別異生不能現起，因此起此勝定果色色，定通凡聖。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未五、辨界別2　申一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科辨界別，分別三界色法的差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：欲、色二界實物有色，何差別耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：欲界的實有色，與色界的實有色，有什麼差別呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、答2　酉一、辨2　戌一、舉色界色3　亥一、清淨最勝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科辨，分辨，又分二科；第一科舉色界色，舉出色界色，又分三科；第一科清淨最勝，色界色是屬於清淨最勝的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：色界諸色清淨最勝，能發光明。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：色界天的色法，很清淨沒有染污，最殊勝，他們的色法能發光明。欲界的色沒有光明，是有質礙的色法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、極微細</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科極微細，色界色極微細。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又極微細，下地諸根所不行故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又色界天光明的色法非常的微細，這是指他們的果報，生到色界天以後，果報色是非常光明微細，是欲界人的眼耳鼻舌身根不能緣慮的。若是色界天人變現色法要令欲界人能見的話，他會變現粗一點的，讓欲界的人看到。如果是他們自己本身的身體，是很微細的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、無有苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無有苦，色界天人的色身無苦受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又無有苦，依彼諸色苦受不生故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又如果生到色界天去，是沒有苦受了。色界天人的色身不生病，所以沒有苦受。欲界的人色身苦受很多，有頭痛、腳痛、手痛、各種病苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、翻例欲界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科翻例欲界，反過來欲界色不清淨、不微細，又有諸多苦受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="54p4325"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">欲界不爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　欲界眾生的色身既不光明，也不微細，又有諸多苦受，與色界眾生不同。欲界的人苦受多樂受少，大部分的人多少都會有一點病痛，心念不同果報也隨之不同。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是說明欲界、色及色界色法的差別相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、總束六相2　午一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科總束六相，將色蘊歸納成六種相狀來觀察，分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出有六相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，色蘊略由六相應知。一、自相，二、共相，三、能依所依相屬相，四、受用相，五、業相，六、微細相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，要略而言，色蘊可以歸納成六相。一、自相，二、共相，三、能依所依相屬相，四、受用相，五、業相，六、微細相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、隨釋6　未一、自相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，隨著列出來的六相，各別解釋，分六科；第一科自相，解釋各類色法不共於它法的自相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">自相者，謂地等以堅等為相，眼等以各別清淨色為相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色蘊的自相，是指地大是以堅為自相，水以濕為自相，火以煖為自相，風以動為自相。自法不共於它法的相狀，名為自相。眼、耳、鼻、舌、身等有各別的屬於自類的清淨色為自相，這是屬於自相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、共相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科共相，色蘊共同的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">共相者，謂一切色皆變礙相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色蘊的共相，是指一切色法都是變礙相，都是剎那變化佔有空間。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、能依所依相屬相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科能依所依相屬相，說明造色由四種而成，互相繫屬的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能依所依相屬相者，大種為所依，造色是能依。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色蘊的能依所依相屬相，指以地水火風四大種為所依，四大種所造的造色為能依，它們是互相繫屬的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、受用相2　申一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科受用相，分二科；第一科標，標出為內色處有所受用增上力，外色境界差別而生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="54p4326"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">受用相者，為內色處有所受用增上力故，外色境界差別而生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色蘊的受用相，是指為了內色處的內根，眼耳鼻舌身根，必須有所受用，由此強而有力的增上力，才會變現出外塵的色聲香味觸。從這一點可以了知，外境是依著有情的受用而有的，而有情受用境界，並不離開這一念心，由此可見三界唯心，萬法唯識的道理真實不虛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有色聚唯有堅生，或唯有濕、或唯有煖、或唯有動、或和合生，為欲隨順內諸色處受用差別故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有時有情的內色處有受用的需求，而生起了有堅固性的色聚；或唯有濕性的水，眾生需要喝水，世間就有水了；或唯有煖性的火，或唯有流動性的風；或有依地水火風不同的組合而生出種種的色法；或者是由堅和濕合在一起，或者煖和風合在一起等等，地水火風中的二種、或三種、乃至四種合在一起，變現出來各種的色法，會有這些不同色法出現，都是為了隨順內身的需要受用這些境界，眼耳鼻舌身需要受用這些境界，就有種種的境界差別現前了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未五、業相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科業相，地水火風四大種各有功能作用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">業相者，謂地等諸大種，以依持、攝受、成熟、增長為相。復有餘業，後當廣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色蘊的業相，是指地水火風各有不同的功能作用，比如地大能作為根身及萬物的依止；水大能攝受，使色聚和合在一起；火大能成熟食物；風大能增長風力發電等，各有不同的功能作用。地水火風還有其他不同作用，後文將詳細說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》復有餘業後當廣說者：如下廣說：地界能為打觸變壞業、建立業、與依止業、違損業、攝受業。水界能為流潤業、攝持業、溉灌業、違損業、攝受業。火界能為照了業、成熟業、燒然業、違損業、攝受業。風界能為發動業、隨轉業、消燥業、違損業、攝受業應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　地水火風四大種各有功能業用，如下文詳細說明：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、地界的業用有打觸變壞業、建立業、與依止業、違損業、攝受業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1、 打觸變壞業：屬於堅硬的這一類色法，能夠敲打、接觸、變化、破壞，比如以鐵為武器可以打仗，地大堅硬能觸摸得到，透過打觸也能使色法變壞。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2、 建立業：堅硬的色聚，比如木石等能建造房子，又人體的骨架主要由地大建立而成。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3、 與依止業：能夠作為有情的依止，比如大地，是一切地居有情及器世間的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　4、 違損業：地界也有違損的作用，如地震能危害人命等。</span></span></span></div>
